machine
NOTE ON USAGE ÓÃ·¨: Compare machine, tool, etc. ÊÔ±È½Ïmachine¡¢ toolµÈ´Ê. A machine consists of moving parts powered by electricity, etc and is designed for a specific job. *machineÊÇÓÉµçÁ¦µÈÇı¶¯µÄ»úÆ÷, ÊÇÎª×öÄ³ÖÖ¹¤×÷¶øÉè¼ÆµÄ. An (electrical) appliance is a machine used in the house, such as awashing-machine or dishwasher. *(electrical) applianceÊÇ¼ÒÓÃµçÆ÷, ÈçÏ´ÒÂ»ú»òÏ´µú»ú. An apparatus is a system of connected machines, wires, etc *apparatusÊÇÏàÁª½áµÄ»úÆ÷¡¢ µ¼ÏßµÈÏµÍ³: the apparatus for lighting the stage ÎèÌ¨ÕÕÃ÷Éè±¸. A tool is an object held in the hand, often used by people in their jobs, eg a hammer, drill or spanner. *toolÊÇÊÖ³Ö¹¤¾ß, ³£Îª¸É»î¶ùµÄÈËÓÃµÄ, Èç¡¡×Ó¡¢ ×ê»ò°â×Ó. An instrument is a tool designed for a technical task, eg a surgeon's knife. *instrumentÊÇÎª¼¼Êõ¹¤×÷Éè¼ÆµÄ¹¤¾ß, ÈçÊÖÊõµ¶. It may have some moving parts and be used in a technical operation, eg a microscope or meter. *instrument¿ÉÄÜÓĞÄ³Ğ©ÔË×ª²¿¼ş²¢ÓÃì¶¼¼Êõ²Ù×÷, ÈçÏÔÎ¢¾µ»òÒÇ±í. An implement is a tool generally used outdoors, especially in gardening or farming, eg a plough, rake or spade. *implementÊÇÍ¨³£ÓÃì¶»§ÍâµÄ¹¤¾ß, ÓÈÖ¸Ô°ÒÕ»òÅ©×÷ÖĞÓÃµÄ, Èç¡¡¡¢ °Ò»òÇÂ. Device and gadget are more general terms. *deviceºÍgadget´ÊÒå½ÏÁıÍ³. Device is often used implying approval of a useful machine or instrument *device³£º¬°ıÒå, Ö¸Ä³»úÆ÷»ò¹¤¾ßºÜÓĞÓÃ´¦: a labour-saving device Ê¡Á¦µÄÆ÷¾ß *  a clever device for locking windows Ëø´°µÄÁéÇÉ×°ÖÃ.
